\doxysubsubsection{Detailed Description}
Include \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{type__precision_8hpp}{glm/gtc/type\+\_\+precision.\+hpp}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} to use the features of this extension.

Defines specific C++-\/based qualifier types.
